When the pinhole is reached, the fluid can\nbe injected into the skin as if from a hypodermic syringe.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Immediately after the\ninjection, the person experiences only a slight stinging sensation and may not\nthink much about it. Several hours later, however, the wound begins to throb\nand severe pain begins. By the time a doctor is seen, it is often too late, and\nthe individual loses a finger or entire arm.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Unfortunately, this\nkind of accident is not uncommon. To reduce the chances of this type of injury,\nrun a piece of wood or cardboard along the hose (rather than fingers) to detect\nthe leak Coat cylinder rods with protective lubricants to avoid rusting. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Failure of the system\ncould cause damage to vessel, personnel and cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Personnel using\nhydraulic equipment should be fully conversant with the proper procedures for\nits safe operation. Operating instructions should be followed at all times.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Operators should ensure\nthat the pressures shown on a gauge is within the operating parameters set by\nthe manufacturer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When the equipment is\nin use, operators should never reach through a linkage of any hydraulically\noperated mechanism to set, adjust or operate the controls.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only authorized\npersonnel should undertake repairs to the equipment or adjustment of the\npressure settings of safety devices. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The equipment should\nnot be operated if it is in any way faulty without prior permission from the\nChief Engineer who must ensure further operations will not compromise safety.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The operator should\nensure that all pressures have been released prior to disconnecting any line,\nplug, etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only use manufacturers'\nrecommended grades of hydraulic fluid.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Keep oil clean. Follow\nmanufacturers' maintenance schedules for changing filters. Efficiency of\nhydraulic systems is directly related to cleanliness.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Leaks add to danger by\ncausing slippery decks and accidents.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Any spillage of\nhydraulic fluid should be cleared up immediately. Some fluids are based on\nmineral oils and any such fluid on the skin should be thoroughly and quickly\nwashed off.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Since vapors from\nhydraulic fluid may be flammable, naked lights should be kept away from\nhydraulic equipment being tested or serviced. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hydraulic leakages to\ndeck can easily run off into the sea and cause pollution. The entire crew\nshould know how to use the emergency stop button. Leaks should be promptly\nreported to the responsible officer. Every effort shall be made to quickly stem\nany leaks. Spillages should be quickly cleaned.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Accumulators are\ndesigned to store oil under pressure when the hydraulic pump cannot keep up\nwith demand, when the engine is shut down, or when the hydraulic pump\nmalfunctions. Even though the pump may be stopped or an implement disconnected,\nthe system is still under pressure. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Always\nrelease pressure first. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Use the company\nchecklist.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Avoid servicing the\nhydraulic system while the machine engine is running. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before disconnecting\noil lines, relieve all hydraulic pressure and discharge the accumulator. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use a non-volatile\ncleaning solvent to wash parts<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pressure relief valves\nthat are maintained, cleaned and tested regularly help avoid dangerous pressure\nbuildups. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Keep contaminants from\nhydraulic oil and replace filters regularly. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">SAFETY IS THE RESPONSIBILTY OF THE ENTIRE CREW LIST -- NOT JUST 4 STRIPERS OR THE SHORE SUPERINTENDENT. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-5-VIi47QVVo/T_QjcsFy0KI/AAAAAAAANME/iG0bSwmavzY/s1600/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-5-VIi47QVVo/T_QjcsFy0KI/AAAAAAAANME/iG0bSwmavzY/s320/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p> </o:p></span></div>\n</o:p></span>\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">29 years in command.</span></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "2", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7033176173598462347/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4891711677722591876", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-07-04T00:54:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-08-31T19:29:54+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTM1NzIzOTk0MzIxCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/07/king-cobra-and-snake-temples-of-kerala.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4891711677722591876", "title": "KING COBRA AND SNAKE TEMPLES OF KERALA- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ctPV40aaZOA/T_NAwFXnF7I/AAAAAAAANHY/Ltc6_V0XhZI/s1600/cghjj.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ctPV40aaZOA/T_NAwFXnF7I/AAAAAAAANHY/Ltc6_V0XhZI/s1600/cghjj.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong><span style=\"color: blue;\">KING COBRA AND SNAKE\nTEMPLES OF KERALA-&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span></strong></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During my honeymoon\nthree decades ago we were at Mysore zoo. There I saw a King Cobra in a enclave.\nThe particulars of the snake indicated that it was 18.1 feet long.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At that time my wife\nremarked, our snake is bigger than that.</span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Naturally I demanded to\nknow \" What the hell do you mean by our snake?\"</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then she told me that\nin her tharavadu ancestral house at Kannur, they had a resident pet King Cobra.\nNobody knew how old it was. It made weekly rounds at a particular time , and\nthose days they kept the external scuppers clean.</span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The huge bungalow was\nset in 6 acres of land, and 1 acre in one corner , went to the snake , living\ninside the roots of a huge tree, which had an Nagakal idol. That entire grove\nwas full of dense bushes creepers, vines and plants. Nobody went that side.\nSometimes he used to come inside the house in the back area, and nobody\ndisturbed it.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The lore was that the snake was guarding a manikyam ( precious\nstone ). If the snake comes and gives this stone to you voluntarily, then you\nare blessed, as this luminous stone had extremely high value.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RdCArPqm114/T_NGgWERvPI/AAAAAAAANJk/QrCUYop3yp0/s1600/180px-Sarpa-Kavu-3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RdCArPqm114/T_NGgWERvPI/AAAAAAAANJk/QrCUYop3yp0/s1600/180px-Sarpa-Kavu-3.jpg\" width=\"240\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then when my wife was\nabout to deliver my elder son, she went to her home at Kannur, as per our\ncustoms and culture. One day I had gone to meet her. She told me to watch out\nfor the King , as his weekly rounds was due. So there I was in the verandah\nkeeping a hawks eye for a slithering reptile. And suddenly there he was, &nbsp;taking his rounds\n, like the lord of all he surveys, along with a sudden increase of twitter of\nbirds. It was easy to identify the huge guy, as its tail was truncated by about 3\ninches, and was not pointed.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At that time I told my\nwife \" I am gonna kill the guy\" --more to see her reaction. And I\nfound she got red faced and hoppin' mad with me, and told me never --ever-- ever --never to talk that way.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then few days before\nshe delivered the baby , she went to the Sarpa Kavu ( Snake Temple ) of Kannur\nto offer eggs and milk to the Cobras there. The King Cobra does NOT belong to\nthe genre of Cobras, as he eats them for breakfast.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This episode I have\nmentioned in one of my posts.Punch into Google search GRATITUDE, THE NOBLEST OF\nALL VIRTUES- VADAKAYIL.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">100 years ago, Kerala\nhad 30000 Snake temples. Today hardly 5000 are left. All these Snake Temples\nhave been destroyed and the land used for building houses. Usually a Hindu will\nnever build his house in an area which had a snake temple. So usually this land\nwas sold to Muslims and Christians.&nbsp; Subdivision and fragmentation of huge plots\nof land, at the time of dividing property between children of deceased parents,\nhad done so much of harm to Kerala.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zh-bDbt7P3A/T_NGq98e5MI/AAAAAAAANJs/kSrJ3wBHsow/s1600/snake-shrine_1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zh-bDbt7P3A/T_NGq98e5MI/AAAAAAAANJs/kSrJ3wBHsow/s320/snake-shrine_1.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">These snake temple\nlands were left alone. Nobody went that side for thousands of years, even to\ncollect firewood. When people wanted rare herbs they kept a piece of Kayam/\nHing/ Asafoetida in their pockets , collected the stuuf in the daylight and\ncame out in a jiffy. The ground is fungus laden and full of rare ferns. Snakes\nof Kerala do NOT bite you unless you step on them or corner them. So these\ngreen pockets all over Kerala, usually with a waterbody or pond,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>has the richest of flora and Ayurvedic herbs.\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">I would suggest to the Kerala Government of Kerala NOT to allow destruction of\nHindu snake temples</span>.</span> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QlJhCWCsNi0/UybGHNh-1NI/AAAAAAAAqag/Dasuc8mHXyg/s1600/02ki_sacred-gro_r3eb02_1571631e.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"256\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QlJhCWCsNi0/UybGHNh-1NI/AAAAAAAAqag/Dasuc8mHXyg/s1600/02ki_sacred-gro_r3eb02_1571631e.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The atheist communists and the Christian and Muslim MLAs\nand Ministers make fun of the superstitious Hindu. I do hope they understand\nthe environmental impact, and look at it from this perspective. The mountain\nsoil and climate of Western Ghats cannot sustain the Ayurvedic medicinal herbs\n, which require the soil and climate of the plains.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Kph39UjSw-0/T_NA5wo9V7I/AAAAAAAANHg/4ghPzzxLB-I/s1600/mnrOTK001.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"425\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Kph39UjSw-0/T_NA5wo9V7I/AAAAAAAANHg/4ghPzzxLB-I/s400/mnrOTK001.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The huge forest at the\nborders of Kerala, Karnataka and Tamil Nadu was full of Sandal wood trees. The\nsmugglers made merry and literally eliminated the Sandal Wood tree, till a\ndreaded and violent bandit by the name of Veerappan , took refuge in these\nforests. For two decades nobody had the guts to steal Sandalwood, with deadly\nVeerappan and his vicious gang on the prowl. The Sandal wood forests became\nlush and abundant all over again. Now that Veerappan is dead and gone, same old\nstory. If you view this with commonsense the snakes in a Sarpa Kavu , are the\nequivalent of Veerappan.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>The venomous\nsnakes<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>kept the greedy man away and did\nNOT allow him to rape that virgin grove of eco-system.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; The King in turn\nate these snakes to maintain the eco-balance.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ekLyEt4lY8U/T_NCn6lu_hI/AAAAAAAANIw/uuaEW_o5t6M/s1600/imagesCAIPW6HG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"452\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ekLyEt4lY8U/T_NCn6lu_hI/AAAAAAAANIw/uuaEW_o5t6M/s1600/imagesCAIPW6HG.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Kerala was created by\nwarrior saint Parashurama , the 6th incarnation of Lord Vishnu, who threw his\naxe ( scalar weapon ) and reclaimed the land from the Varuna , the Arabian sea.\nKerala is a narrow strip of land between the sea and the Western ghat\nmountains. This land which was reclaimed was salt laden and not fertile.\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; That whole\narea has white fragrant Mandara flowers. There are 30000 snake idols in this\ngrove. Rather this regal snake is worshipped as a God. If a King Cobra\nis killed accidentally, it is cremated with ghee. A king Cobra can curse a man.\nI have seen this happening. Our school was the house of a very rich man (\nSadanandan of Calicut . This building is now Calicut telephones ) . When he\nmade his house he was advised by astrologers to leave the Sarpa kavu at the\ncorner of the plot alone. He himself took his gun and blasted off a lot of\nsnakes and set fire to the area. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-clxz5OSYc0E/UybGtjIIjOI/AAAAAAAAqbA/GXFCEcECKcw/s1600/P10hesh00583.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-clxz5OSYc0E/UybGtjIIjOI/AAAAAAAAqbA/GXFCEcECKcw/s1600/P10hesh00583.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">His entire family went to ruin within a couple\nof years. Some contacted incurable skin diseases, some went raving mad. The\nlast was a forlorn woman who used to sit outside the gates of our school , all\nalone like a beggar, with her cloth bundle. You could make out that she was\nquite fair and attractive in her young age.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\nIn the Mahabharata 4000 BC, Arjuna and Lord Krishna set fire to the great and ancient Khandava forest , so that they could build their Indraprastha palace . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DWmYnkfLW0Y/T_1CSXXkDcI/AAAAAAAANmA/NITlMh0pDvo/s1600/wgjjj.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"262\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DWmYnkfLW0Y/T_1CSXXkDcI/AAAAAAAANmA/NITlMh0pDvo/s400/wgjjj.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nEverything living in the forest died, except Maya Danava ( he was saved and then arm twisted to show gratitude by designing the amazing Indraprasta hall . He also designed the&nbsp;Mayan calendar later ) , 4 birds ( Sarngakas ) and Aswasena, the son of the Naga king Takshaka.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jOcLdzUsdGw/T_1Cdt8NRRI/AAAAAAAANmI/J9BrovzNT8M/s1600/chhh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"398\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jOcLdzUsdGw/T_1Cdt8NRRI/AAAAAAAANmI/J9BrovzNT8M/s400/chhh.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAswasena later tried to take revenge for his mother, and hid in the quiver of Karna who was fighting Arjuna still like an arrow, but Arjuna's charioter Lord Krishna prevented this dart from hitting Arjuna by causing the horses to bend down&nbsp;thus sinking the chariot wheels.&nbsp;.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pOluJOMjJ1I/T_1Dj3Yig3I/AAAAAAAANmQ/JqWdzysMu2U/s1600/imagesCA0WCJ0O.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-pOluJOMjJ1I/T_1Dj3Yig3I/AAAAAAAANmQ/JqWdzysMu2U/s400/imagesCA0WCJ0O.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n60 years after the Mahabharata war, Takshaka had his revenge by killing Parikshit, Arjuna's grandson. Parikshit was forewarned and so he build a tower in the midle of a lake, with every hole and crevice plugged. But Takshaka coverted itself into a worm and bore into a mango, which was to be taken in a basket as food. Parikshit was engulfed in flames due to the potency of the venom--as a poetic justice , as Takshaka's wife was killed in the Khandava forest fire.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-evyfQknICc8/T_09yLNglQI/AAAAAAAANlY/DvAW4h8T198/s1600/taxaka_statue.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-evyfQknICc8/T_09yLNglQI/AAAAAAAANlY/DvAW4h8T198/s320/taxaka_statue.jpg\" width=\"213\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: red;\">Picture above shows King Cobra Takshaka , his wife who dies in the Khandava forst fire and his son Aswasena</span></em> </div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Peralassery\nSubramanya Temple, is located 15 kms from Kannur . The temple<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>has a shrine for the serpent God and has a number of bronze and copper\nidols of snakes . On Nag Panchami day. This festival is observed on the\nfifth day of Shravana month of Hindu lunar calendar after the amavasya of\nAshada month.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NrLRuaslxNs/T_NCRLoez9I/AAAAAAAANIo/yoeF3fws1FY/s1600/SarpaKavu.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"524\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NrLRuaslxNs/T_NCRLoez9I/AAAAAAAANIo/yoeF3fws1FY/s1600/SarpaKavu.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Women fast the previous day. They then take\nbath at dawn and pray at the Sarpa kavu . Immediately Lord Krishna trapped him. \"Let a palatial Sabha (meeting hall) as thou choosest, be built by thee, if thou, O son of Diti, who art the foremost of all artists, desirest to do good to Yudhishthira the just (Mahabharata.2.1)\".</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Krishna told Arjuna \"Your city has been constructed by Vishwakarma and is truly beautiful. However, the Indraprastha palace is much too plain for such a wonderful city. Let a palatial meeting hall be constructed for Yudhishtra the just. Maya Danava is the best person to construct it, being the architect of the Asuras.\"</span></div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_64B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_64MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<b><span style=\"color: magenta;\">KRISHNA WAS ALREADY SETTING UP THE INCIDENT OF KING DURYODHANA FALLING INTO A POOL OF WATER , QUEEN DRAUPADI LAUGHING LOUND IN SARCASM\u2014WHICH WAS THE TRIGGER FOR THE MAHABHARATA WAR.</span></b></div>\n<br />Maya measured out a plot of land five thousand cubits square and began the construction. Today we have just around 4500 snake groves and they are disappearing fast. \u2026\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nSnakes keep away animals and rodents whose excreta degrades the humus \u2026\u2026\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nIn humus, carbon frequently outweighs nitrogen by 10 to one\u2026\u2026.. Humpless western cow dung has too much nitrogen\u2026\u2026\u2026..<br />\n<br />\nHumic acid increases water retention, retains nutrients and enhances microbiological activity, enzymes in soil, etc\u2026\u2026. The organic matter on biodegradation is converted in to humus, which contains humic and fulvic substances. \u2026..<br />\n<br />\nThe humic substance contains various functional groups of carboxylic, carbonyl, phenolic, alcoholic with higher molecular weight of 40,000 to 70,000 and higher cation exchange capacity (100-130 meq/100 gm). Lignite contains more of humic acid\u2026..---<br />\n<br />\nAt some point, all of the good stuff in the organic matter is used up and some molecules remain that can\u2019t be used by micro-organisms or plants\u2026.. This remaining material is called humus. \u2026\u2026\u2026<br />\n<br />\nIt consists mostly of carbon and so it is still organic, but micro-organisms just can decompose it any further\u2026\u2026\u2026. Humus is so stable that it can persist in the soil for hundreds of years\u2026<br />\n<br />\nHumus has a negative charge which means that many of the nutrients plants require stick to humus, including ammonium (source of nitrogen), calcium, magnesium and phosphorous to name a few\u2026\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nThe humus sponge holds onto these nutrients and prevents rain from washing them away. \u2026.. When a plant root comes in contact with it, the plant root is able to remove the nutrients from the humus sponge. \u2026\u2026\u2026The process is a bit more complicated than this, but you can think of humus as being a slow release source of fertilizer for your plants\u2026..<br />\n<br />\nThe most important reason for having humus is that it is responsible for aggregation. \u2026\u2026 Aggregation is what makes soil loose and very friable, improving the structure of soil\u2026.. Better soil structure found in humus rich soil makes it easier for plant roots to grow by providing them with better access to nutrients, water and most importantly oxygen\u2026\u2026<br />\n<br />\nHumus is a colloidal substance, and increases the soil's cation exchange capacity, hence its ability to store nutrients by chelation. \u2026.While these nutrient cations are accessible to plants, they are held in the soil safe from being leached by rain or irrigation..<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2--</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; This remaining material is called humus. \u2026It consists mostly of carbon and so it is still organic, but micro-organisms just can decompose it any further\u2026\u2026 Humus is so stable that it can persist in the soil for hundreds of years.<br />\n<br />\nHumus has a negative charge which means that many of the nutrients plants require stick to humus, including ammonium (source of nitrogen), calcium, magnesium and phosphorous to name a few\u2026<br />\n<br />\nThe humus sponge holds onto these nutrients and prevents rain from washing them away. \u2026.. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/06/the-deep-state-and-shadow-government_28.html?showComment=1530255759317#c1413190284692248433\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">June 29, 2018 at 12:32 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_66MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 1--<br />\n<br />\nThe biochemical structure of humus enables it to moderate \u2013 or buffer \u2013 excessive acid or alkaline soil conditions\u2026<br />\n<br />\nHUMUS IS DECIMATED BY CHEMICAL FERTILISERS. \u2026<br />\n<br />\nMOST OF THE FARMER SUICIDES IN INDIA IS 100% DUE TO LOSS OF HUMUS IN THE SOIL. \u2026.<br />\n<br />\nAPCO MODI IS TOO BUSY ANGLING FOR A NOBEL PRIZE FROM ZIONIST JEWS TO UNDERSTAND ALL THIS. .<br />\n<br />\nTAMIL NADU MUST UNDERSTAND THIS INSTEAD OF CRYING LIKE RETARDED BABIES FOR CAUVERY WATER\u2026<br />\n<br />\nRECENTLY OUR LOSER LAWYER TURNED COLLEGIUM JUDGES ( BOTTOM DREGS OF THE SCHOOL CEREBRAL BARREL ) BANNED BURNING OF CROP STUBBLE ( WHICH PRODUCES BIOCHAR ) BECAUSE OF DELHI SMOG\u2026<br />\n<br />\nIF THIS IS THE CASE SHIFT THE CAPITAL OF INDIA TO A PLACE WHERE THERE IS NO TEMPERATURE INVERSION\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nBiochar has the ability to sequester carbon out of the atmosphere and back into the ground ..<br />\n<br />\nTall grasses burn quick and hot, however, close to the ground where the roots start, air is excluded so the base of the grasses will pyrolyze and not burn\u2026<br />\n<br />\nCarbon is the most essential element of soil fertility. When organic matter is added to agricultural soils to increase carbon levels, most of it rapidly decomposes to carbon dioxide and escapes to the atmosphere...<br />\n<br />\nOnly a very small percentage eventually becomes stable humic matter... Humification takes decades to centuries..The process creates a fine-grained, highly porous charcoal that helps soils retain nutrients and water\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nBiochar serves as an electron buffer for redox reactions and helps bacteria swap electrons among themselves, improving their metabolic efficiency as a microbial community.. ..<br />\n<br />\nWith its pores and its electrical charges, biochar is capable of both aBsorption and aDsorption.. ..<br />\n<br />\nThe surfaces of biochar, both internal and external, aDsorb materials by electro-chemical bonds, working like an electric sponge...<br />\n<br />\nBiochar surfaces adsorb carbon and retain it in compounds with minerals, supporting at the same time a large microbial community that potentially makes more efficient use of organic debris containing carbon and other nutrients...<br />\n<br />\nUnlike biochar, compost is quickly broken down by microbial action in soil over months to at most, decades, depending primarily on climate...<br />\n<br />\nBiochar lasts at least ten times longer in most soils.... Biochar is effective at retaining nitrogen in soils and there is NO need for CHEMICAL UREA...<br />\n<br />\nThe desh drohi GREEN REVOLUTION has left us with a rapidly deteriorating climate, and soils that are dying and eroding.... Biochar, as a form of recalcitrant carbon, is the medicine that DELIBERATELY degraded and unproductive Indian top soils need....<br />\n<br />\nIndia was blessed with HUMUS laden topsoil with healthy microbes and earthworms for millions of years....<br />\n<br />\nJust 55 years of desh drohi GREEN REVOLUTION has decimated our holy topsoil...<br />\n<br />\nTHIS IS THE ONLY INTELLIGENT WAY TO PREVENT FARMER SUICIDES...<br />\n<br />\nThe desh drohi GREEN REVOLUTION has caused our holy topsoil to lose 80% of their original soil organic carbon (SOC) pool...<br />\n<br />\n90% of our lakes have disappeared due to artificial nitro fertIliser overuse. ..<br />\n<br />\nALL ABOVE HAS BEEN SENT TO MODI AND HIS MINISTERS MORE THAN 30 TIMES..<br />\n<br />\nWHO CARES ?..<br />\n<br />\nMODI GIVES US MORE AND MORE JAANKARI ABOUT GANDHI AND BR AMBEKDAR ..<br />\n<br />\nYESTERDAY MODI WAS RECITING SOME KABIRDAS SHLOKA (&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">EXAMPLE: Pascal\u2019s triangle has many unusual properties and a variety of uses:</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Horizontal rows add to powers of 2 (i.e., 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The horizontal rows represent powers of 11 (1, 11, 121, 1331, 14641) for the first 5 rows, in which the numbers have only a single digit.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Adding any two successive numbers in the diagonal 1-3-6-10-15-21-28\u2026 results in a perfect square (1, 4, 9, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">It can be used to find combinations in probability problems (if, for instance, you pick any two of five items, the number of possible combinations is 10, found by looking in the second place of the fifth row. Do not count the 1\u2019s.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">When the first number to the right of the 1 in any row is a prime number, all numbers in that row are divisible by that prime number</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The Fibonacci Series is found in Pascal\u2019s Triangle.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Pascal\u2019s Triangle, is formed by starting with an apex of 1. Every number below in the triangle is the sum of the two numbers diagonally above it to the left and the right, with positions outside the triangle counting as zero.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The numbers on diagonals of the Pascalstriangle add to the Fibonacci series</span><br /><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XMriWTvPXHI&amp;pbjreload=10</span></span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The Fibonacci numbers are--</span><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">0, 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 13, ... (add the last two to get the next)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The golden section numbers are--</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">0\u202261803 39887... = phi = \u03c6 and</span><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">1\u202261803 39887... = Phi = \u03a6</span><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The golden string is</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; All on board except the essential watchkeepers witness the ceremony--almost like a wedding.<br />\n<br />\nThe \"landlubber\" has to drink King Neptunes toast--which could be a mixture of various edible liquids , including sea water, beer, coffee, Tabasco chilly sauce, raw eggs etc. After drinking one cup of this concoction he is supposed to ask for more , like how Oliver twist asked Mr.Bumble for more gruel.<br />\n<br />\nHe is dunked into the ship's swimming pool after a nice haircut and annointed by some cosmetics ( paint ). Raw eggs are broken on his head for shampoo.<br />\n<br />\nKing Neptune , after he is satisfied with the initiation ceremony, now formally baptises the \"land lubber\" into a \"sea dog \" by poking him with his trident.<br />\n<br />\nThen we have sport competitions like running, tug of war, sack race , wheel barrow race etc--with handsome cash prizes.<br />\n<br />\nAt night there will be a grand party.At sea, the equator is calm and there are not too many ships around. <br />\n<br />\nThe new \"sea dogs\" are given the Equator crossing ceremony passing certificates by the Captain. <br />\n<br />\nYou can recognise these souls in a jiffy, because their heads will be clean shaven.
